**1))** 1) kennen, wissen, eine Kenntniss von Etwas oder Jmd haben; erkennen, innewerden, merken, kennen lernen, erfahren: *yathāmī anyo anyaṃ na jānan*

**sense-1-gram-note-cow)** [AV. 10,1,25.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av10.001.html#av10.001.25) Nach [P. 1,3,76](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/76) und [VOP. 23,58](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mugdhabodha/app1?23,58) med., wenn das obj. in näherer Beziehung zum subj. steht: *gāṃ jānīte* er kennt seine Kuh
[P.], Sch. Ist die nähere Beziehung durch ein anderes Wort angegeben, so kann sowohl act. als med. stehen nach
[P. 1,3,77.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/77) *svāṃ gāṃ jānāti* oder *jānīte*

- **RU:** [AV. 10,1,25.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av10.001.html#av10.001.25) По [P. 1,3,76](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/76) и [VOP. 23,58](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mugdhabodha/app1?23,58) med., когда obj. находится в более тесной связи с subj.: *gāṃ jānīte* он знает свою корову
[P.], Sch. Если более тесная связь обозначена другим словом, то возможно как act., так и med. — согласно
[P. 1,3,77.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/77) *svāṃ gāṃ jānāti* или *jānīte*
  <sub>attested</sub>

**1)** — desid. *jijñāsate*
[P. 1,3,57.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/57)
[VOP. 23,57.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mugdhabodha/app1?23,57) ep. auch act.
 1) zu kennen —, zu wissen —, zu erkennen —, kennen zu lernen begehren; untersuchen, prüfen, auf die Probe stellen: *hāsaṃ te — jijñāsāmi* ich verlange zu wissen worüber du lachst
[R. 2,35,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?2,35,19) *jijñāsantau parāṃ gatim*
[4,60,6.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?4,60,6) *dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānām*
[M. 2,13.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?2,13)
[P. 1,3,57](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/57), Sch.
*yāvanna jijñāsata ātmatattvam*
[BHĀG. P. 5,5,5.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?5,5,5) *jijñāsita* was man kennen zu lernen gewünscht hat
[1,5,3.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?1,5,3) [4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?1,5,4) *jijñāsamāno rāmasya vīryam*
[MBH. 3,8660.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.8660) *dhanuṣastasya vīryaṃ hi jijñāsantaḥ*

**8)** — 8) nach *anujñāta*, wenn es ein Lob einschliesst, ist das nachfolgende Wort im comp., so wie auch ein nachfolgendes verbum finitum, unbetont, gaṇa *kāṣṭhādi* zu [P. 8,1,67.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/8/1/67)
[68.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/8/1/68)

- **RU:** — 8) после *anujñāta*, когда оно включает похвалу, следующее слово — в comp., равно как и следующий за ним verbum finitum, — безударно, gaṇa *kāṣṭhādi* zu [P. 8,1,67.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/8/1/67)
[68.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/8/1/68)
- **EN:** — 8) according to *anujñāta*, when it includes a commendation, the following word is in the comp., and likewise a following finite verb is unaccented, gaṇa *kāṣṭhādi* to [P. 8,1,67.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/8/1/67)

## abhyanujñā

`j_y_a~~h0_04_a_byanu`


**1)** — *abhyanu*

**3)** — 3) sich erinnern dass; mit blossem fut. st. des imperf., oder mit *yad* und imperf.; wenn die Erinnerung sich auf zwei mit einander in Verbindung stehende Ereignisse erstreckt, kann sowohl mit als ohne *yad* imperf. oder fut. stehen.

- **RU:** — 3) вспоминать, что; с простым fut. st. imperf., или с *yad* и imperf.; если воспоминание относится к двум взаимосвязанным событиям, может стоять как с *yad* imperf. или fut., так и без него.

- **EN:** — 3) to recall, remember that; with bare fut. st. of the imperf., or with *yad* and imperf.; when the recollection extends to two events connected with each other, it may stand either with or without *yad* imperf. or fut..

## nisjñā (nis+jñā)

`j_y_a~~h0_19_nis`


**1)** — *nis* unterscheiden, bestimmen; herausfinden, auffinden: *na haiveha svau cana pāṇī nirjānīyuḥ*
[ŚAT. BR. 4,2,1,2.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?4,2,1,2) *śvo nodeti* (*candraḥ*) *abhrasya vā hetoranirjñāya vai*
[11,1,4,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?11,1,4,1) *vidyudvai vidyutya vṛṣṭimanupraviśati sāntardhīyate tāṃ na nirjānanti*
[AIT. BR. 8,28.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?8,28)

- **RU:** — *nis* различать, определять; выяснять, обнаруживать: *na haiveha svau cana pāṇī nirjānīyuḥ*
[ŚAT. BR. 4,2,1,2.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?4,2,1,2) *śvo nodeti* (*candraḥ*) *abhrasya vā hetoranirjñāya vai*
[11,1,4,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?11,1,4,1) *vidyudvai vidyutya vṛṣṭimanupraviśati sāntardhīyate tāṃ na nirjānanti*
[AIT. BR. 8,28.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?8,28)
- **EN:** — *nis* to distinguish, determine; to find out, discover: *na haiveha svau cana pāṇī nirjānīyuḥ*

## prajñā (pra+jñā)

`j_y_a~~h0_22_pra`


**1)** — *pra* erkennen, verstehen: insbes. den Weg oder die Richtung oder auch die Art und Weise eines Verfahrens erkennen, Etwas zu finden wissen, sich zurechtfinden, Bescheid wissen, sich orientiren: *pra nīcīragne aruṣīrajānan*
[ṚV. 1,72,10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv01.072.html#rv01.072.10) *pra pitṛyāṇaṃ panthāṃ jānāti*
[AV. 8,10,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av08.010.html#av08.010.19) [20.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av08.010.html#av08.010.20) [15,12,5.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av15.012.html#av15.012.05) *tvayā lokamaṅgirasaḥ prājānan taṃ lokaṃ puṇyaṃ pra jñeṣam*
[9,5,16.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av09.005.html#av09.005.16) *tato vai te pra yajñamajānanpra svargaṃ lokam* (vgl. *svargaṃ lokaṃ na prajānāti mūḍhaḥ*
[P. 1,3,76](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/3/76), Sch.) [AIT. BR. 2,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?2,1)
*te devā na kiṃ canāśaknuvankartuṃ na prājānaṃste 'bruvannaditiṃ tvayemaṃ yajñaṃ prajānāmeti*

[ŚAT. ## anuprajñā (anupra+jñā)

`j_y_a~~h0_23_anupra`


**1)** — *anupra* nach Jmd sich zurechtfinden, — den Weg finden: *yajñena vai devā ūrdhvāḥ svargaṃ lokamāyaṃste bibhayurimaṃ no dṛṣṭvā manuṣyāśca ṛṣayaścānuprajñāsyantīti*
[AIT. BR. 2,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?2,1) auffinden: *jyotiranu prajānan*
[ṚV. 3,26,8.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv03.026.html#rv03.026.08) *na haitaṃ daivamātmānamanuprajānīyāt*
[ŚAT. BR. 7,4,2,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?7,4,2,19)

- **RU:** — *anupra* ориентироваться вслед за кем-либо, находить путь: *yajñena vai devā ūrdhvāḥ svargaṃ lokamāyaṃste bibhayurimaṃ no dṛṣṭvā manuṣyāśca ṛṣayaścānuprajñāsyantīti*
[AIT. BR. 2,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?2,1) находить, обнаруживать: *jyotiranu prajānan*
[ṚV. 3,26,8.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv03.026.html#rv03.026.08) *na haitaṃ daivamātmānamanuprajānīyāt*
[ŚAT. BR. 7,4,2,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?7,4,2,19)
- **EN:** — *anupra* to find one's bearings by someone, to find the way: *yajñena vai devā ūrdhvāḥ svargaṃ lokamāyaṃste bibhayurimaṃ no dṛṣṭvā manuṣyāśca ṛṣayaścānuprajñāsyantīti*
[AIT. BR. 2,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?2,1) to find, discover: *jyotiranu prajānan*
[ṚV. 3,26,8.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv03.026.html#rv03.026.08) *na haitaṃ daivamātmānamanuprajānīyāt*
[ŚAT. BR. 7,4,2,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?7,4,2,19)

## abhiprajñā (abhipra+jñā)

`j_y_a~~h0_24_a_bipra`


**1)** — *abhipra* an Jmd denken, für Jmd sorgen: *tamaśanāyāpipāse abrūtāmāvābhyāmabhiprajānīhīti*
[AIT. UP. 2,5.]
[SĀY.] ergänzt *adhiṣṭhānam* und ererklärt *abhi˚* durch *cintaya* denke aus.

- **RU:** — *abhipra* думать о ком-либо, заботиться о ком-либо: *tamaśanāyāpipāse abrūtāmāvābhyāmabhiprajānīhīti*
[AIT. UP. 2,5.]
[SĀY.] дополняет *adhiṣṭhānam* и объясняет *abhi˚* посредством *cintaya* помысли.
- **EN:** — *abhipra* to think of someone, to care for someone: *tamaśanāyāpipāse abrūtāmāvābhyāmabhiprajānīhīti*
[AIT. UP. 2,5.]
[SĀY.] supplies *adhiṣṭhānam* and explains *abhi˚* by *cintaya* think out.
  <sub>attested</sub>

**4)** — 4) behaupten, aussagen, statuiren, annehmen: *ke yūyaṃ puṣpavantaśca — bibhrataḥ kṣātramojaśca brāhmaṇyaṃ pratijānatha* wie könnt ihr behaupten, dass ihr Brahmanen seid?
[MBH. 2,842.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?2.842) *ityetatpratijānāmi*

[RĀJA-TAR. 3,180.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/rajatar/app1?3,180)

- **RU:** — *saṃvi* обращаться к кому-л. (gen.) увещевать, советовать: *ādau pravartite cakre tathaivādiparāyaṇe . vartasva puruṣavyāghra saṃvijānāmi te 'nagha ..*
[MBH. 12,2451.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.2451) — caus. возвещать, провозглашать: *atha kṛtvā kṣaṇācchlokametaṃ taṃ saṃvyajijñapat*
[RĀJA-TAR. 3,180.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/rajatar/app1?3,180)
- **EN:** — *saṃvi* to encourage, advise Jmd (someone) (gen.): *ādau pravartite cakre tathaivādiparāyaṇe . vartasva puruṣavyāghra saṃvijānāmi te 'nagha ..*
[MBH. 12,2451.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.2451)
  <sub>attested</sub>

**2)** — caus. kundmachen, hersagen: *atha kṛtvā kṣaṇācchlokametaṃ taṃ saṃvyajijñapat*
[RĀJA-TAR. 3,180.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/rajatar/app1?3,180)
- **EN:** — caus. to make known, to recite: *atha kṛtvā kṣaṇācchlokametaṃ taṃ saṃvyajijñapat*
[RĀJA-TAR. 3,180.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/rajatar/app1?3,180)

## samjñā

`j_y_a~~h0_34_sam`


**1)** — *sam*
 1) eines Sinnes sein, einträchtig sein; sich vertragen, sich einigen: *saṃ vo manāṃsi jānatām*

## abhisamjñā

`j_y_a~~h0_35_a_bisam`


**1)** — *abhisam* einverstanden sein in Bezug auf (acc.), sich Etwas gern gefallen lassen: *payo ha vai prajā jātā abhisaṃjānate vijigyānaṃ mā prajā śriyai yaśase 'nnādyāyābhisaṃjānāntā iti*
[ŚAT. BR. 2,6,3,6.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?2,6,3,6) *svamevaitadrasamabhisaṃjānate*
[5,4,3,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?5,4,3,19) *indraṃ devā jyaiṣṭhyāyābhisamajānata*
[TS. 2,2,11,6.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/taittiriyas/app1?2,2,11,6)

- **RU:** — *abhisam* быть согласным относительно (acc.), охотно соглашаться с чем-л.: *payo ha vai prajā jātā abhisaṃjānate vijigyānaṃ mā prajā śriyai yaśase 'nnādyāyābhisaṃjānāntā iti*
[ŚAT. BR. 2,6,3,6.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?2,6,3,6) *svamevaitadrasamabhisaṃjānate*
[5,4,3,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?5,4,3,19) *indraṃ devā jyaiṣṭhyāyābhisamajānata*
[TS. 2,2,11,6.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/taittiriyas/app1?2,2,11,6)
- **EN:** — *abhisam* to be in agreement with regard to (acc.), to gladly accept something: *payo ha vai prajā jātā abhisaṃjānate vijigyānaṃ mā prajā śriyai yaśase 'nnādyāyābhisaṃjānāntā iti*

## jñā

`j_y_a~~h1_00_pwg00`


**2)** *jñā*
- **EN:** *jñā*

**2.1)** 1) _adj._ am Ende eines comp. kennend, kundig; s. *ṛtajñā, pada˚* und vgl. *jña* .
- **EN:** 1) _adj._ at the end of a comp. "knowing, acquainted with, skilled in"; s. *ṛtajñā, pada˚* and vgl. *jña*.

**2.2)** — 2) _f._ = *ājñā* mit abgeworfenem Anlaut in Folge eines vorangehenden *e* oder *o: te jñayā* [MBH. 1,3168.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.3168) *sainyasya vrajato jñayā* [3,16308.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.16308)
- **EN:** — 2) _f._ = *ājñā*, with the initial sound dropped as a consequence of a preceding *e* or *o: te jñayā* [MBH. 1,3168.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.3168) *sainyasya vrajato jñayā* [3,16308.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.16308)

 1) *iti samyaṅmayā jñātaṃ prabhurjānātyataḥ param* so v. a. der Fürst weiss, was er jetzt zu thun hat,
[KATHĀS. 103,81.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?103,81) *jāne mahāṭavīṃ kāṃcitpraviṣṭā nikhilā vayam* ich weiss, ich erinnere mich, dass
[69,34.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?69,34) *ka evaṃ jānīte* mit folgendem fut. wer weiss, ob nicht
[Spr. 3573.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?3573) *naitā jānanti pitaraṃ na kulaṃ na ca mātaram* sie wissen nichts vom Vater u. s. w. so v. a. sie achten nicht des Vaters u. s. w.
[1646.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?1646) sich erinnern, mit gen.: *hṛdayaṃ tatra jānāti kartuścaiva kṛtasya ca*
[MBH. 12,5169.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.5169) annehmen, als bekannt voraussetzen
[Spr. 2491.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?2491) [5227.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?5227) halten für: *khalagiraṃ jānāti satyām*
[2858.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?2858) *svajanaiḥ svātmavajjanturjñāyate guṇavānparaiḥ*

- **RU:** *jñā*, *jña = jānīhi*

 1) *iti samyaṅmayā jñātaṃ prabhurjānātyataḥ param* так v. a. государь знает, что ему теперь надлежит делать,

[1646.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?1646) помнить, вспоминать, с gen.: *hṛdayaṃ tatra jānāti kartuścaiva kṛtasya ca*

- **EN:** *jñā*, *jña = jānīhi*
[BHĀG. P. 10,89,46.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bom/app1/?10,89,46)
 1) to know, *iti samyaṅmayā jñātaṃ prabhurjānātyataḥ param* so v. a. "the prince knows what he now has to do",
[KATHĀS. 103,81.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?103,81) *jāne mahāṭavīṃ kāṃcitpraviṣṭā nikhilā vayam* "I know, I remember that"
[69,34.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?69,34) *ka evaṃ jānīte* with a following fut. "who knows whether not"
[Spr. 3573.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?3573) *naitā jānanti pitaraṃ na kulaṃ na ca mātaram* "they know nothing of their father" u. s. w. so v. a. "they pay no heed to their father u. s. w."
[1646.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?1646) "to remember", with gen.: *hṛdayaṃ tatra jānāti kartuścaiva kṛtasya ca*
[MBH. 12,5169.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.5169) "to assume, to presuppose as known"
[Spr. 2491.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?2491) [5227.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?5227) "to hold to be, to regard as": *khalagiraṃ jānāti satyām*
[2858.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?2858) *svajanaiḥ svātmavajjanturjñāyate guṇavānparaiḥ*
[3324.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?3324) *jajñe* pass.
[RĀJA-TAR. 5,481.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/rajatar/app1?5,481) *yadyaśakyamiti jñātvā* "holding to be impossible"
[Spr. 4833.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?4833) [Sp. 137, Z. 11. fg.] the passage
[PAÑCAT. V,7](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app1?5,7) is to be deleted, since there *jātavinaṣṭāḥ* is to be read instead; vgl.
[Spr. 1461.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?1461) [Z. 19] read *pūrṇametaddhi* instead.

## jñā

`j_y_a~~h0_zz_pw00`


**1)** **1.** √*jñā*, *jānāti, jānīte* (episch auch *jāna˚* st. *jānī˚*); √*jña* = *jānīhi* [BHĀG. P.]
- **EN:** **1.** √*jñā*, *jānāti, jānīte* (epic also *jāna˚* st. *jānī˚*); √*jña* = *jānīhi* [BHĀG. P.]

**1a)** — 1〉 ohne Object oder mit Acc.
- **EN:** — 1) without an object or with Acc.

**1a-a)** — a〉 kennen, wissen, bekannt —, vertraut sein, Kenntniss haben von, erkennen, — an (Instr. [235,19](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?235)), in Erfahrung bringen, forschen nach, inne werden, merken, kennen lernen, erfahren. *jāne* (eingeschoben) das weiss ich [133,29](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?133). *ka evaṃ jānīte* mit folgendem Fut. wer weiss, ob nicht [Spr. 546](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?546). Mit einer Negation Nichts wissen von auch so v. a. keine Rücksicht nehmen auf und nicht theilhaftig werden. *jñāta* bekannt, gekannt, von dem oder wovon man Etwas weiss, erkannt, bemerkt, kennen gelernt, erfahren.
- **EN:** — a) to know, have knowledge of, be acquainted —, familiar with, have knowledge of, recognise, — by (Instr. [235,19](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?235)); to ascertain, search for, become aware of, notice, get to know, learn, experience. *jāne* (parenthetic) "that I know" [133,29](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?133). *ka evaṃ jānīte* with following Fut. "who knows whether not" [Spr. 546](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/boesp1/app1/?546). With a negation "to know nothing of", also so v. a. "to pay no heed to and not partake of". *jñāta* "known, acknowledged, that of which or about which one knows something, recognised, noticed, become acquainted with, experienced".

**1a-b)** — b〉 anerkennen, gutheissen, billigen.
- **EN:** — b) to acknowledge, approve, sanction.

**1a-c)** — c〉 als das Seinige anerkennen, in Besitz nehmen (buddh.).
- **EN:** — c) to recognise as one's own, take possession of (buddh.).

**1a-d)** — d〉 kennen —, erkennen als, wissen —, inne werden —, merken, dass; mit doppeltem Acc.
- **EN:** — d) to know —, recognise as, be aware —, perceive — that; with double Acc.

**1a-e)** — e〉 Etwas annehmen, supponiren, meinen (*mayā jñātam* ich war der Meinung [KĀD. 2,60,3]), ansehen —, halten für; mit doppeltem Acc. *mṛṣā* Etwas für unwahr halten [308,13](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?308). *jñāta* gehalten für (Nom.), — von (*Gen.).
- **EN:** — e) to assume, suppose, hold the opinion (*mayā jñātam* "I was of the opinion" [KĀD. 2,60,3]), regard —, consider as; with double Acc. *mṛṣā* "to consider something untrue" [308,13](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?308). *jñāta* "considered as" (Nom.), — "of" (*Gen.).

**1a-f)** — f〉 Jmd vertraulich aufsuchen.
- **EN:** — f) to visit someone confidentially.

**1b)** — 2〉 mit Gen.
- **EN:** — 2) with Gen.

**1b-a)** — a〉 kennen, — lernen.
- **EN:** — a) to know —, get to know.

**1b-b)** — b〉 sich erinnern.
- **EN:** — b) to remember.

**1b-c)** — c〉 *Med. wohl es zu thun haben —, sich abgeben mit [235,15. fgg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?235) *śambhormukunde jānīte* soll = *śaṃbhunā sādhanena mukunde pravartate* sein.
- **EN:** — c) *Med., probably "to have to do with —, engage with" [235,15. fgg.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?235); *śambhormukunde jānīte* is said to = *śaṃbhunā sādhanena mukunde pravartate*.

**1c)** — 3〉 mit Infin. verstehen zu.
- **EN:** — 3) with Infin. "to understand how to".

**1d)** — Caus. *jñāpayati, ˚te* und *jñapa˚*; Partic. *jñapta* und *jñāpita*.
- **EN:** — Caus. *jñāpayati, ˚te* and *jñapa˚*; Partic. *jñapta* and *jñāpita*.

**2)** — 1〉 Act.
- **EN:** — 1) Act.

**2-a)** — a〉 unterweisen, belehren.
- **EN:** — a) to instruct, teach.

**2-b)** — b〉 in Kenntniss setzen, benachrichtigen [ĀŚV. GṚHY. 4,7,2].
- **EN:** — b) to inform, notify [ĀŚV. GṚHY. 4,7,2].

**2-c)** — c〉 zu wissen —, kund thun, mittheilen, verkünden, lehren.
- **EN:** — c) to make known —, announce, communicate, proclaim, teach.

**2-d)** — d〉 Jmd mit Etwas bekannt machen, mit doppeltem Acc.
- **EN:** — d) to make someone acquainted with something, with double Acc.

**2-e)** — e〉 Jmd (Gen.) berichten, dass; mit doppeltem Acc.
- **EN:** — e) to report to someone (Gen.) that; with double Acc.

**2f)** — 2〉 Med. angehen, bitten, zusprechen; mit Acc. der Person.
- **EN:** — 2) Med. "to approach, ask, address"; with Acc. of the person.

**3)** — Desid. *jijñāsate* (episch auch Act.)
- **EN:** — Desid. *jijñāsate* (epic also Act.)

**3-1)** — 1〉 zu kennen, — zu wissen —, Kenntniss zu haben von —, zu erkennen —, kennen zu lernen wünschen, untersuchen, prüfen, auf die Probe stellen. *jijñāsyāmas* wohl fehlerhaft für *jijñāsāmas*.
- **EN:** — 1) to wish to know —, to be acquainted with —, to have knowledge of —, to recognise —, to wish to get to know; to investigate, examine, put to the test. *jijñāsyāmas* is probably an error for *jijñāsāmas*.

**3-2)** — 2〉 sich erkundigen nach, sich Gewissheit verschaffen über.
- **EN:** — 2) to inquire about, to obtain certainty about.

**3-3)** — 3〉 vermuthen.
- **EN:** — 3) to surmise.

**4)** — Desid. vom Caus. **jijñāpayiṣati*, **jijñāpa˚* und *jñīpsati* Jmd mit Etwas bekannt machen wollen; mit doppeltem Acc.
- **EN:** — Desid. from Caus. **jijñāpayiṣati*, **jijñāpa˚* and *jñīpsati* "to wish to make someone acquainted with something"; with double Acc.

**5)** — Mit *ati* scheinbar [BHĀG. P. 12,3,28](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bom/app1/?12,3,28), wo aber *itijānīhi* zu lesen ist.
- **EN:** — With *ati* apparently [BHĀG. P. 12,3,28](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bom/app1/?12,3,28), but where *itijānīhi* is to be read instead.

**anu)** — Mit *anu*
- **EN:** — With *anu*

**anu-1)** — 1〉 Etwas verstatten, gewähren, vergönnen, zugestehen, zusagen, gutheissen, billigen.
- **EN:** — 1) to allow, grant, permit, concede, promise, approve, sanction something.

**anu-2)** — 2〉 (logisch) anerkennen [Comm. zu NYĀYAS. 1,1,40].
- **EN:** — 2) (logically) "to acknowledge" [Comm. zu NYĀYAS. 1,1,40].

**anu-3)** — 3〉 befolgen, zur Richtschnur nehmen.
- **EN:** — 3) to follow, take as a guideline.

**anu-4)** — 4〉 Jmd (Gen.) Etwas nachsehen, verzeihen.
- **EN:** — 4) to overlook —, forgive someone (Gen.) something.

**anu-5)** — 5〉 Jmd (Acc.) ermächtigen, eine Erlaubniss ertheilen (mit Dat. eines Nom. act. oder mit **prati* und Acc. eines Nom. act.). *anujñāta* ermächtigt, der eine Erlaubniss erhalten hat.
- **EN:** — 5) to authorise —, grant permission to someone (Acc.) (with Dat. of a Nom. act., or with **prati* and Acc. of a Nom. act.). *anujñāta* "authorised, one who has received permission".

**anu-6)** — 6〉 Jmd (Acc.) erlauben fortzugehen, verabschieden, entlassen. *ratham* einen Wagen entlassen, so v. a. fortfahren heissen.
- **EN:** — 6) to permit someone (Acc.) to depart, to dismiss, send away. *ratham* "to dismiss a carriage"; so v. a. "to bid drive on".

**anu-7)** — 7〉 Etwas verabschieden, so v. a. Lebewohl sagen, verzichten auf [R. 2,42,8](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?2,42,8).
- **EN:** — 7) to take leave of something; so v. a. "to say farewell, renounce" [R. 2,42,8](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?2,42,8).

**anu-8)** — 8〉 sich Jmd (Acc.) gnädig erweisen, seine Gewogenheit an den Tag legen.
- **EN:** — 8) to show oneself gracious to someone (Acc.), to display one's favour.

**anu-9)** — 9〉 scheinbar Jmd bitten, beschwören [R. 2,21,28](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?2,21,28), wo aber mit der [ed. Bomb.] *sāhaṃ nānujānāmi* zu lesen ist.
- **EN:** — 9) apparently "to beg —, entreat someone" [R. 2,21,28](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?2,21,28), but where [ed. Bomb.] *sāhaṃ nānujānāmi* is to be read instead.

**anu-atm)** — Caus.

- **EN:** — With *samā* "to recognise, get to know, notice, become aware that" (with double Acc.). *˚jñāta* "known —, acknowledged as" (Nom.); at the end of a Comp. dass. ([Comm. zu NYĀYAS. 1,1,22]) and "whereby something is recognised".

- **EN:** — Desid. in *upajijñāsya*.

- **EN:** — With *praṇi* "to consider, reflect upon" [BHAṬṬ.]

- **EN:** — With *nis* "to distinguish, determine, find out, discover" [ṚV. 3,31,4](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv03.031.html#rv03.031.04).

- **EN:** — With *vinis* dass.

- **EN:** — With *pari* "to notice, recognise, get to know, ascertain, make sure of, know precisely; recognise as" (with double Acc.). *˚jñāta* "known"; at the end of a Comp. "known as".

**sam-caus)** — Mit *pra* erkennen, unterscheiden, verstehen; insbes. den Weg, die Richtung oder die Art und Weise eines Verfahrens erkennen, Etwas zu finden —, Bescheid wissen, sich orientiren; gewahr werden, wissen, erfahren von, ausfindig machen. Mit der Negation Nichts wissen von auch so v. a. die Bedeutung von — nicht kennen. *prajñāta* bekannt, gewöhnlich, bekannt als (Nom.).
- **EN:** — With *pra* "to recognise, distinguish, understand"; insbes. "to know the way, direction, or manner of a procedure, to find something —, know one's way about, orient oneself; become aware of, know, learn of, find out". With the negation "to know nothing of", also so v. a. "not to know the meaning of". *prajñāta* "known, usual, known as" (Nom.).

**ni-1)** — Mit *vi*

- **RU:** — С *vi*
— 1〉 распознавать, знакомиться, разузнавать, разведывать, замечать, воспринимать, осознавать, слышать, — что (с двойным Acc. или с *yad*), узнавать —, учиться у (Gen.), обретать или иметь верное познание, различать, иметь уверенность, узнавать что-либо в чём-либо (Loc.) — видеть, знать, что, (с двойным Acc.).

**ni-1-neg)** — Mit *na* und Inf. nicht wissen, was — heisst, nie in den Fall kommen zu. *vijñāyate* es ist bekannt, — anerkannt, es wird gelehrt. *mā vijñāyi* mit einem Vorangehenden Nom. bei Grammatikern es werde darunter nicht — verstanden, so v. a. man sehe dieses nicht als — an.

- **RU:** — С *na* и Inf. не знать, что значит, никогда не оказываться в положении. *vijñāyate* известно, — признано, этому учат. *mā vijñāyi* с предшествующим Nom. у грамматиков под этим не следует понимать, так v. a. этого не следует считать за.
- **EN:** With *na* and Inf. not to know what — means, never to come into the situation of. *vijñāyate* it is known —, acknowledged, it is taught. *mā vijñāyi* with a preceding Nom., in grammarians, it is not to be understood as —; so v. a. this is not to be regarded as —.
  <sub>lexicographic</sub>

**ni-2)** — 2〉 zu wissen thun, verkünden [BHĀG. P.]

- **RU:** — 2〉 давать знать, возвещать [BHĀG. P.]
- **EN:** 2) to make known, proclaim [BHĀG. P.]

- **EN:** Caus. 1) to make something known, proclaim, report, voice one's opinion, announce — ([RĀJAT. 3,241](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/rajatar/app1?3,241)), to declare —, say that (with double Acc.).

- **RU:** — 2〉 с Acc. лица доводить до понимания кого-либо, наставлять, давать знать, ставить в известность, говорить —, сказать кому, обращаться с просьбой или вопросом, — относительно (*˚artham, prati* или Dat.).
